    <h1>Goldman Sachs and GitLab</h1> 
    <p>Goldman Sachs improves from bi-monthly builds to over a thousand per day.</p> <a href="/customers/goldman-sachs/" class="btn cta-btn orange margin-top20">Read the case study</a>

      <img src="/images/case_study_logos/BI_Worldwide_case_study_logo.svg" class="solution-logo" alt="BI Worldwide logo" width="230"> 
      <h3>Increasing deployments to 10 times a day</h3> 
      <p class="customer-lead">BI Worldwide Corporate Product Development Team removed technology barriers to focus on building microservices.</p> 
      <div class="btn-group"> <a href="/customers/bi_worldwide/" class="btn cta-btn orange margin-top20">Read More</a> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="col-md-6 col-md-offset-1"> 
      <div class="annotated-image-container"> 
       <img src="/images/customers/paessler-spot-image.jpg" class="u-rounded" alt="Gitlab BI Worldwide spot image jpg"> 
       <div class="annotation annotation--sw"> 
        <div class="annotation-content"> <strong>10x</strong> daily deploys 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="row u-margin-top-lg"> 
     <div class="col-md-12"> 
      <blockquote class="customer-quote"> 
       <div class="quote-meta"> <cite class="quote-attribution"> Adam Dehnel <span class="quote-attribution-title">Product Architect</span> </cite> 
       </div> 
       <div class="quote-body"> 
        <p class="quote-text"> “One tool for SCM+CI/CD was a big initial win. Now wrapping security scans into that tool as well has already increased our visibility into security vulnerabilities. The integrated Docker registry has also been very helpful for us. Issue/Product management features let everyone operate in the same space regardless of role.” </p> 
       </div>
